Still very pleasant to walk around the complex with all the trees, flowers, lake, swans & ducks, but it breaks your heart to see the weeds taking over everywhere and there is what once would have been a beautiful Rose Flower path and the roses are still flowering but no maintenance at all and weeks are taller than the rose bushes and all they seem to do is just the grass and forget the rest.

Rooms and facilities were very clean, so I was impressed.

Room layout is excellent and very, very big with a courtyard and external spa, you start to relax as soon as you walk in the door. The only thing that put me and my wife off is the mahjong table in the main room on the first floor.

TV had no movies and no English Chanels at all.

Food in the All Day Dining (Chinese Restaurant) was very nice but limited.

Breakfast was not a very big selection and probably because it is not peak season, however it also was not very good and put us off even trying the Western Food for dinner and went across the road for fast food instead.

Staff were very nice and polite.

We want  for my wife's birthday and apart from the impressive building structures, there was no WOW factor for the overall experience.

msg:This is both an evaluation of Chengdu Songpin Hotel and a comparison post of the three major luxury hotels in Chengdu.
Chengdu Qingcheng Songpin Hotel, Chengdu Diaoyutai Hotel, Qingcheng Six Senses Hotel. This time I spent five days experiencing these three hotels.

Facilities: Qingchengshan Songpin Hotel has the largest area and the most complete facilities in the same price range. Basic room types have their own private hot springs. Although the indoor swimming pool is not open, the overall facilities are very complete, whether it is in-room facilities or outdoor facilities. The Diaoyutai Hotel is a bit dated. The facilities are well maintained, but the carpets need further cleaning. Six Senses hotel infrastructure is also available.
Hygiene: Songpin's hygiene is very good.
Environment: Songpin and Six Senses are good.
Service: Song Pin, available at any time and responsive to all requests. Six Senses takes a long time to communicate when there are requests, and there are many restrictions on children's breakfast. The service is the best! !
Housekeeper Dong Wei.

msg:I took my family's elderly to Qingcheng Mountain for fun on the weekend and stayed at Qingcheng Songpin Hotel.
Environment: The hotel is located opposite Sunac City in the suburbs of Dujiangyan. It covers a large area and has an artificial lake. The greenery and natural environment are excellent. Although it is an average of more than 20 minutes' drive from Qingcheng Mountain and Dujiangyan, there are all kinds of facilities around, and there is no problem with food, clothing, housing and transportation. (There are amusement parks, water worlds, ice and snow cities, etc. nearby. It is suitable for parents and children to pass the time)

Facilities: The private bath of Lanyue is basically the same as the photos in the promotion. There are lazy chairs, humidifiers and mini bars. The sofa bed can sleep two people. The bathtub is a little troublesome. The hot water is not stable. For this reason, I specially found a housekeeper and solved it in time. Of course, I also want to complain about the private bath. The hot spring pool is pre-filled with water, with a constant temperature of 41 degrees. It is very comfortable to soak in at night. It is just that the fallen leaves in the yard and some floating catkins on the trees are spread out, but it can be understood. After all, there are trees, wind and birds in the courtyard, which is still very comfortable.
Hygiene: No obvious dead corners were found, the hotel was cleaned up, welcome fruit and night bed service were provided, the second floor lounge chair was a little stained, but the flaws were not enough, thanks to the cleaning ladies.
Service: Special thanks to the housekeeper Huang Xiaoyu for her warm hospitality. Although I am more accustomed to self-sufficiency, she still helped a lot. After adding WeChat, the hotel was centered on the guests in all matters big and small. Then the hotel's door-to-door service was very timely. The mahjong machine was broken and the door-to-door service was fast. The mineral water was delivered in a timely and accurate manner, and the shuttle bus staff was also very enthusiastic.

An impressive hotel experience, very comfortable, thank you!
